<div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-hzl789qpmo5s" data-node="hzl789qpmo5s">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text"><em>Spirit House illuminates the spiritual and spectral boundaries between life and death</em></span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-bs4e0rlq8ifm text-size-x-small" data-node="bs4e0rlq8ifm">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>A major survey at the Cantor Arts Center showcases an intergenerational range of emerging and established contemporary visual artists of Asian descent.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-jcgx9a4f7r8d" data-node="jcgx9a4f7r8d">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>The<a href="https://museum.stanford.edu/" target="_self">Cantor Arts Center</a> presents <em><a href="https://museum.stanford.edu/exhibitions/spirit-house" target="_self">Spirit House</a></em><em>,</em> a major group exhibition foregrounding how contemporary artists of the Asian diaspora challenge the boundary between life and death through art. On view from Sept. 4, 2024, to Jan. 26, 2025, the exhibition comprises nearly 50 works of art by 33 artists, including large-scale paintings, digital media, ceramic sculpture, photography, and significant new acquisitions within the museums permanent collection.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-s7ok9z8rywnd" data-node="s7ok9z8rywnd">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">

			<a href="https://news.stanford.edu/stories/2024/09/spirit-house-illuminates-the-spiritual-and-spectral-boundaries-between-life-and-death" target="_self" class="fl-button">
							<span class="fl-button-text">More on Spirit House</span>
						<i class="fl-button-icon fl-button-icon-after SArts-Arrow" aria-hidden="true"></i>
			</a>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-pbuo7qf1y2wi" data-node="pbuo7qf1y2wi">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text"><em>Encounters: Where Creative and Scientific Inquiry Meet</em></span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-l7cygd06o8zs text-size-x-small" data-node="l7cygd06o8zs">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>A new limited series podcast from Denning Visiting Artist Janani Balasubramanian</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-yo915vzcp4ar" data-node="yo915vzcp4ar">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p data-pm-slice="1 1 []">What happens when art meets science? Stanford alumni and host Janani Balasubramanian returns to campus to explore the dynamic intersection of these two disciplines throughout their residency in the <a class="ProsemirrorEditor-link" href="https://arts.stanford.edu/office-of-the-vice-president-for-the-arts/visiting-artist-fund/">Denning Visiting Artist Fund</a>. Discover how interdisciplinarity drives breakthrough, from the physics of the interstellar medium to the myths of ancient times, featuring leading researchers and innovators.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-utp80f3ylxac" data-node="utp80f3ylxac">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-button-wrap fl-button-width-auto fl-button-left">

<div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-50drys47nfc3" data-node="50drys47nfc3">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text"><em>From Sea to Studio</em></span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-s1dkne25muh4 text-size-x-small" data-node="s1dkne25muh4">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Doerr School of Sustainability Visiting Artist collaborates with Oceans researchers at Hopkins Marine Station</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-fwq85pvmuls4" data-node="fwq85pvmuls4">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p data-pm-slice="1 1 []">A new visiting artist program at Stanford is bringing together a sculptor and ocean scientists to create a sculpture based on the Southern Ocean ecosystem. Their collaboration aims to raise awareness of the impact of human activity on the environment.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-vraulw9n3siq" data-node="vraulw9n3siq">

Art is essential to Stanford and we represent its evolving multitudes and influences. As we welcome students and colleagues for a new year, were energized to support and showcase the extraordinary range of craft, curation, and interdisciplinary innovation that is only possible here.
